				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Jesu, der du meine Seele, BWV 78 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>7 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1724 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>For the 14th Sunday after Trinity.
</p>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Commentary_on_the_movements">Commentary on the movements</span></h4>
<ol><li>Chorus: Jesu, der du meine Seele. An expressively chromatic passacaglia with many episodes of free counterpoint. The soprano, above this, sings the chorale tune unadorned. 
</li><li>Aria (Soprano, Alto): Wir eilen mit schwachen, doch emsigen Schritten. A deliciously contrasting and vivacious duet. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Tenor): Ach! ich bin ein Kind der Sünden. Secco recitative. 
</li><li>Aria (Tenor): Das Blut, so meine Schuld durchstreicht. An aria with obbligato flute at its most characteristic. This movement is distinctive thanks to its rising scale patterns and frequent leaps. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Bass): Die Wunden, Nägel, Kron und Grab. Recitative with string accompaniments.
</li><li>Aria (Bass): Nur du wirst mein Gewissen stillen. A dance-like movement characterized by a flowing oboe line interupted by initial chords <i>alla francese</i>. 
</li><li>Chorale: Herr, ich glaube, hilf mir Schwachen. A plain chorale setting. 
</li></ol>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Print_Sources_Consulted">Print Sources Consulted</span></h4>

</li></ul>
<dl><dd>Oxford: Oxford University Press, 2005.
